50 lvl is 15000 xp.

\r\n\t\t\t\tNone of this is confirmed information, it's just some random reddit post that blew up for some reason. Chrome extensions are not open source by default.

Even if it's true (which, tbh, is most likely the case), it's nothing new. Virtually every website uses google analytics these days, and that's basically the same - just on a larger scale.

I mean sure, it shouldn't happen, but it doesn't surprise me, and I don't see why this huge shitstorm is happening now. It's like all these people only now realised that privacy in the surface web is not a thing.\t\t\t

\r\n\t\t\t\tBtw, incase some of you have seen that my profile is private, here's the explaination. Sometimes, I get dozens of invitations from random people, mostly scammers, and it just annoys the hell out of me. Therefore, I change my profile status to "Friends Only", so that I can enjoy a day or more with no friend requests from random people trying to scam me. I always change it back to "Public" after a few hours, a day or even two.
Hope there are no misunderstandings \t\t\t

Well thats pretty easy! If someone do not want to be part of BLS anymore, well okey than, he can leave! Boom Thats It! We go on and getting more elitish and special!
========================================================================
Sort of. If someone leaves because they want to start their own group or whatever, that's fine. But to leave and then, within almost hours, throws hints that they "May want to come back", well, no, because I do not have time for "wishy-washy" people..

And I say that because, you, of all people, know just how many people really want in; want to be here-a waiting list if you will. And I want to be fair to those that have been jumping through our "hoops" and waiting patiently to become part of BLS.

My word of advise to anyone is to think long and hard before you click on the "leave group" button, because there will be no turning back.
